--para--\*form.du="0" \*form.fid="Ia39dc160181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3" \*p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51" Agreement madeon [date of agreement], between [name of corporation], a nonprofit cooperative corporation organized under the laws of the State of New York, referred to as &ldquo;\'93Corporation,&rdquo;\'94whose principal place of business and address for receiving correspondence regarding this agreement is [address of corporation], [name of city], 
[name of county], [name of state], and [name of producer], of [address of producer], [name of city], 
[name of county], [name of state], [an independent producer/a member of the corporation], referred to as &ldquo;
\'93Producer.&rdquo;\'94--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> In consideration of the following mutual covenants, Corporation and Producer agree as follows:
--para----para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 1. AGRICULTURAL PRODUCTS PURCHASED AND SOLD
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Corporation buys from Producer and Producer sells to Corporation all [specification of products], referred to as &ldquo;\'93products,&rdquo;\'94produced by or for Producer or acquired by Producer as landlord or lessor, which products are 
[specification of required attributes of product], except products that Producer reserves for personal use and not for sale. Producer agrees to deliver all such products at places directed by Corporation.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 2. TITLE AND RISK OF LOSS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Corporation and Producer agree that title to all products subject to this agreement shall pass as soon as they have a potential existence. However, risk of loss shall be borne by Producer until delivery.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 3. CENTRAL AGENCY OR SIMILAR ASSOCIATION
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Corporation may exercise any powers conferred on it under this agreement through any central agency of which Corporation and any other similar organization are or may become members.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 4. ADVANCES ON PRODUCTS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Corporation agrees to make such advances to Producer on products delivered under this agreement as in the discretion of its board of directors may be justified by marketing conditions.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 5. MANNER OF DETERMINING PRICE; REVOLVING FUND; POOLS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Corporation agrees to sell, either in the natural or processed state, products delivered by Producer under this agreement, together with the products delivered by other Producers, and to pay over ratably the net amount received therefrom as payment in ful
l to Producer after making deductions:
--para----para--\*<field>fi.lvl="2"</field> (a). 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> to cover advances, interest on advances, costs of picking, gathering, harvesting, receiving, assembling, transporting, handling, grading, packing, inspecting, processing, financing, advertising, storing, insuring, selling, and marketing such products and 
products derived therefrom;
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="2"</field> (b). 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> to cover organization, operating, and maintenance expenses;
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="2"</field> (c). 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> for capital in a central agency;
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="2"</field> (d). 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> to cover a revolving fund retained for the purpose of building up such an amount of capital as may be deemed necessary by its board of directors from time to time; and
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="2"</field> (e). 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> as needed for revolving such capital in the manner that may be provided in the Corporation's bylaws.
--para--The aggregate of such deductions shall not exceed [[percentage of gross sales price]&percnt;%of the gross sales price of such products and products derived therefrom/[number of cents] cents per [bushel/carton/[specification of other unit]]].
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Corporation, within the discretion of its board of directors, is authorized to establish, from time to time, daily, weekly, monthly, or seasonal pools of the agricultural products marketed by it of the same variety, grade, and quality. All Producers havin
g such products in a particular pool shall share ratably in the net amount received therefrom.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 6. DELIVERY OF PRODUCTS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> All products shall be delivered by Producer at the earliest reasonable time after harvesting at such places as Corporation may direct, and with such identification at Producer's expense as may be prescribed by the Corporation.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 7. LOSSES
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Any loss that Corporation may suffer on account of inferior or damaged condition of products at delivery shall be charged against Producer.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 8. ASSOCIATION'S POWER TO ENCUMBER PRODUCTS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Producer further agrees that Corporation or central marketing agency, individually or jointly, shall have the power to borrow money for any purpose of Corporation or central marketing agency on the security of the products delivered to Corporation, the pr
oducts derived therefrom, or on any evidence of such products, byproducts, or cash accounts arising from their sale and to give a lien, either legal or equitable thereon, as the absolute owner. Producer also agrees that Corporation or central marketing ag
ency may grade, pool, or commingle any part of such products or products derived therefrom with other products or products derived therefrom of like grade and variety and shall exercise all other rights of ownership without limitation.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 9. LIQUIDATED DAMAGES FOR PRODUCER'S BREACH OF AGREEMENT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Producer and Corporation agree that this agreement is one of a series dependent for its true value on the adherence of each and all of the contracting parties to all such agreements and that the cancellation of this agreement for the failure of Producer t
o comply with it shall not affect other similar agreements. Producer and Corporation also agree that the remedy at law for any breach of this agreement would be inadequate and that it would be impracticable and extremely difficult to determine the actual 
damage resulting to Corporation should Producer fail to deliver the covered products, regardless of the cost of such failure.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Producer agrees to pay to Corporation as liquidated damages for all products sold, delivered, or withheld by or for Producer's benefit, other than in accordance with the terms of this agreement, [$[dollar amount of liquidated damages for all product]/the sum of $[dollar amount of liquidated damages payable] per [specification of unit] on all products].
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 10. COSTS AND EXPENSES OF LEGAL ACTION
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> If Corporation files an action by reason of a breach or threatened breach of this agreement, Producer shall pay all court costs, costs for bonds and otherwise, expenses of travel and all expenses arising out of or caused by the litigation, and reasonable 
attorney's fees expended or incurred by it in such proceedings, and all such costs and expenses shall be included in the judgment.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 11. INTEGRATION OF CERTIFICATE AND BYLAWS INTO AGREEMENT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> The articles of incorporation and the bylaws of corporation, now or hereafter in effect, and this agreement constitute the entire agreement between Corporation and Producer.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 12. OTHER AGREEMENTS; PRODUCER'S APPLICATION FOR CORPORATION MEMBERSHIP
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Corporation may enter into agreements with other Producers differing in terms from those contained in this agreement but consistent with the bylaws of Corporation without invalidating this agreement, provided that Producer at Producer's request may sign a
similar agreement as a substitute for this agreement. By signing this agreement, Producer, unless already a member, applies for membership in Corporation, and the signing of this agreement by Corporation will constitute an acceptance of such application.

--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 13. STANDARDS AND INSPECTION
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> Corporation or the central agency shall establish or adopt standards for products and shall make rules and regulations governing the product's handling and shipping and shall provide inspectors or graders to grade the products. Producer agrees to be bound
by such grading and to observe such rules and regulations. Association or the central agency shall provide for the inspection of all products delivered under this agreement and, if any such products are not in proper condition for sale, they shall be pre
pared for sale at Producer's expense.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 14. TERMINATION AND RENEWAL OF AGREEMENT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> After this agreement has been in effect [number of years]years from the date of its acceptance by Corporation, either party to the agreement may terminate it in any year on the last day of the anniversary month in which this agreement was so accepted by notifying the other party in writing of this intention, s
uch notice to be given between the [ordinal number of day]and [ordinal number of day]day of the month immediately prior to the effective date of termination. If neither party terminates this agreement in any year, it is mutually agreed that such failure shall constitute conclusive evidence that the parties have renewed this agreement for another year.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 15. PAYMENT OF LIENS ON PRODUCTS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> If there is a lien on any of the products delivered under this agreement, Producer authorizes Corporation or central agency to pay the holder of such lien from the proceeds derived from the sale of such products before any payment is made to Producer unde
r this agreement.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 16. NO OTHER AGREEMENTS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> The parties agree that there are no oral or other conditions, promises, covenants, representations, or inducements in addition to or at variance with any other terms of this agreement and that this agreement represents the voluntary and clear understandin
gs of both parties fully and completely.

--para--Notes to Form--para-- --para--Tax Notes 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> A farmer's cooperative must limit the amount of business itdoes with nonmembers. It may market products or purchase supplies and equipment for nonmembers only if: (i) the value does not exceed the value of the products, supplies, and equipment of members; and (ii) the value of the purchases made for those who ar
e neither members nor producers does not exceed 15&percnt;%of total purchases. \*<field>st.ref.id="I04A9XW"</field> 26 U.S.C.A. &s;\'a7521(b)(4). In addition, buying and selling for its own profit, such as selling by-products of purchases made for members to nonmembers, will disqualify a cooperative, even if sales are minimal.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> This explains the inclusion of a provision like that of Section 12 in the above agreement, which makes the contract itself an application for membership and an acceptance of that application.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|53|32:51"</field> The revolving fund method of financing referred to in Section 5 is a hybrid type of security that has elements of both debt and equity. Because of the dual nature of the certificates of interest that are issued in this fund, they have sometimes been decla
red to be stock and other times indebtedness. See \*<field>rc.ref.id="I09QBCW"</field> Mertens Law of Federal Income Taxation &ss;\'a7\'a734A:1 et seq.for a more complete discussion of the taxation of cooperatives and their patrons.

--para----para--\*<field>fi.lvl="2"</field> 1. 
--para--\*<field>

--para--\*<field>

--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> As a result of those contracts, Corporation will market a large proportion of the crop of [name of fruit], referred to in this agreement as &ldquo;\'93fruit,&rdquo;\'94produced in the State of New York.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="2"</field> 4. 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Packer is in the business of handling, processing, and packaging such fruit and desires to secure an adequate and certain supply of fruit for handling, processing, and packaging and to save the labor and expense of soliciting orders or contracts from the 
individual producers of such fruit.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="2"</field> 5. 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Corporation is empowered to buy and sell the fruit of its members. In consideration of the above and the mutual promises of the parties to this contract, it is agreed as follows:
--para----para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 1. SALE OF FRUIT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> During the term of this contract, Corporation shall sell to Packer for handling, processing, and packaging in its plants, and Packer shall purchase and accept from Corporation for handling, processing, and packaging in its plants such fruit grown by membe
rs of the Corporation as follows:
--para----para--\*<field>fi.lvl="4"</field> A. 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> All such fruit grown by certain members of the Corporation during the [identification of year]season as set forth and identified in Exhibit [designation of exhibit]attached and made a part of this contract.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="4"</field> B. 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> All such fruit grown during the [identification of year]season by the members of the Corporation identified on Exhibit [designation of exhibit]attached and made a part of this contract, except to the extent that such Exhibit [designation of exhibit]may be amended by mutual agreement of Corporation and Packer.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 2. TERM OF CONTRACT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> This contract shall cover the crops of fruit grown during the [designation of season]season and the [designation of season]season.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> &ldquo;\'93Season,&rdquo;\'94as used in this agreement, means that period commencing with the [ordinal number of day]day of [name of month]of one calendar year and ending with the [ordinal number of day]day of 
[name of month]of the following calendar year.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 3. SEPARATE LISTING OF EACH GROWER
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> The ability of Corporation to deliver the fruit hereby sold to Packer is based and dependent on Corporation's crop contract with its grower&ndash;-members. If Corporation is unable to perform this contract because of any failure in performance of any of the provisions of the grower&ndash;-members' contracts to Corporation or by clauses beyond Corporation's direct control, the mutual obligations and terms of this contract will not be affected, changed, or released as to any fruit from any other grower that i
s listed for the current crop year to Packer under this contract. For purposes of this section, each grower herein listed to packers shall be deemed listed to Packer under the terms of this contract separately from every other grower&ndash;-member listed to Packer under the terms of this contract, as though each grower&ndash;-member were covered by a separate contract with Packer.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 4. INABILITY OF PACKER TO PERFORM
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> In case of fire, boiler explosion, interruption of power, strikes or other labor disturbances, lack of transportation facilities, shortage of labor supplies, perils to the city, floods, earthquakes, action of the elements, invasion, war, riot, insurrectio
n, rebellion, interference of civil or military authorities, enactment of legislation, or any unavoidable casualty or cause beyond the Packer's control, affecting the conduct of Packer's business to the extent of preventing or unreasonably restricting, re
ceiving, handling, processing, or packaging operations, including any obligation on Packer's part to transfer the fruit covered by this agreement or to furnish bins therefor, Packer will be excused for performance under this contract during the period that 
Packer's business or packaging operations are so affected. Packer may, during such period, accept such portion of the fruit as Packer has informed Corporation in its judgment it can economically handle.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Packer shall immediately give Corporation written notice of Packer's inability to perform and the specific cause or causes thereof. In any event, Packer shall pay, according to contract, for all fruit received by Packer.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 5. DIVERSION TO OTHER PACKERS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> With respect to the fruit that Packer has advised Corporation of its inability to handle pursuant to Section 4, Corporation retains the right, without liability of any kind or character to Packer, to divert the fruit to a Packer who is able to accept it i
n order to prevent economic waste to the growers and consumers.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 6. FAILURE OF ASSOCIATION TO DELIVER
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If, for the same causes enumerated in Section 4, the farming operations of any grower&ndash;-member of fruit covered by this agreement are so affected that such member or members are unable to make complete delivery of the fruit, Corporation shall make every reasonable effort to complete deliveries under this contract. However, Corporation shall 
be excused from the performance of that part of the contract that it is unable to perform because of these causes during the period the member's farming operations are so affected.

--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Corporation shall not be liable for the failure to deliver fruit destroyed by rain, frost, flood, or other similar casualties.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 7. INDIVIDUAL AGREEMENTS WITH PACKER
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Members of Corporation may enter into individual agreements with Packer with respect to delivery of fruit and advances for growing, harvesting, and other costs as indicated below. The form of the agreements between individual grower&ndash;-members of Corporation and Packer shall be in the form outlined in Exhibit [designation of exhibit]attached and made a part of this contract.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Packer shall furnish to each such grower&ndash;-member a copy of the agreement at the time of its execution.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 8. PAYMENT OF EXPENSES
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Packer shall pay expenses of delivering, weighing, inspecting, and receiving of all fruit subject to this agreement in accordance with its present customs and practices in the industry.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 9. INSPECTION BY ASSOCIATION
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Corporation shall have the right at any time by its authorized agents to examine and inspect any fruit held by Packer on account of Corporation under memorandum receipt or other similar arrangement.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 10. SETTLEMENT STATEMENT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Packer shall furnish to each grower&ndash;-member of Corporation covered by this contract and to Corporation itself at the time of final settlement for fruit delivered under this contract for each crop year a copy of the settlement statement together with financial calculations indicating grower's
returns.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 11. FURNISHING OF BINS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Packer shall use its best efforts to furnish the grower&ndash;-members of Corporation bins in clean and good repair for the purpose of delivering fruit in accordance with its present customs and practices in the industry.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 12. FAILURE TO SUPPLY BINS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If Packer shall neglect or fail to meet the reasonable bin requirements of grower&ndash;-members of Corporation covered by this agreement, Packer shall pay Corporation damages sustained by the grower&ndash;-members and Corporation on account of such neglect or failure.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Packer shall not be liable for damages when Packer cannot supply bins because of strikes, fire, acts of God, or other causes beyond Packer's control and of which notice has been given to Corporation under Section 4 of this contract. Packer shall not be li
able for damages when Packer has allocated bins on a reasonable basis among grower&ndash;-members of Corporation and other growers from which Packer purchases fruit.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 13. QUALITY AND GRADE OF FRUIT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> All fruit delivered under this contract shall be of the quality and grades in effect for such fruit as may be developed and established by Packer or Corporation with approval of the other. In the event Packer establishes various grades by which different 
prices of grade may be paid grower&ndash;-members, Corporation may establish prices for its grower&ndash;-members on the basis of grade in accordance with the provisions of Sections 16 through 22.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 14. COMPLIANCE WITH FAIR LABOR STANDARDS ACT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Corporation guarantees that all of the fruit subject to this contract was or will be produced and delivered in compliance with all applicable standards of the Fair Labor Standards Act (\*<field>st.ref.id="I09QAYM"</field> 29 U.S.C.A. &ss;\'a7\'a7201 et seq.), as amended.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 15. BREACH OF GUARANTIES
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Should Corporation breach any of the guaranties in Sections 13 or 14, Packer may, at its option, refuse to accept delivery. Packer shall have no obligation to pay for the crop, and Corporation may dispose of the crop free of the contract.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 16. TONNAGE TO BE SOLD
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Corporation shall sell to Packer and Packer shall purchase and accept from Corporation the following tonnage of such fruit: [number of tons of fruit]grown by members of Corporation covered by this contract at the price or prices indicated below.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 17. FAILURE TO AGREE ON PRICE
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If the parties to this agreement fail to agree on a price or prices under Sections 18 and 19 of this contract, Packer shall pay and Corporation shall accept for all fruit delivered to Packer by Corporation or the growers it represents a reasonable price, 
as that term is used in Section 18.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 18. ASCERTAINMENT OF REASONABLE PRICE
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> The reasonable price referred to in Section 17 shall be ascertained in the following manner:
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Corporation shall announce an opening price or prices that Corporation believes to be a reasonable price for each variety and grade or grades for any crop year on or before the [ordinal number of day]day of [name of month]of such year. Such announcement shall be made on the basis of consultations with individual packers and an examination by Corporation of all available economic and supply data that influence the sale and purchase price of such fruit.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Packer shall advise Corporation within [number of days]days after receipt of the announced opening price or prices for the [name of fruit]season of its acceptance or rejection of the price or prices. On the acceptance of the announced price or prices by [fraction of packers]in number of packers who purchase fruit from Corporation and those aggregate purchases represent [fraction of estimated total tonnage]of the estimated total tonnage of fruit offered for sale by Corporation under contracts of sale similar to this agreement, such opening price or prices shall be the reasonable price, provided, however, that among the requisite [fraction of packers]
of packers who accept the announced price or prices, there shall be included one Packer whose estimated purchase of fruit tonnage under contract with the Corporation for the season shall be one of the [number of largest estimated tonnages]largest estimated tonnages under contract between Corporation and any purchaser for the season.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> For purposes of the following calculation, Corporation for the [identification of year]season shall refer to the estimated tonnage set forth in Exhibit [designation of exhibit]attached to this contract and similar exhibits to similar agreements with other packers of such fruit. For the [identification of year]season, Corporation shall refer to the list and estimates furnished to Packer and to other packers for the season in accordance with Sections 1 and 2 of this contract and similar agreements.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 19. NONACCEPTANCE OF OPENING PRICE
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If the requisite packers do not signify their acceptance of the announced opening price or prices within [number of days]
days after the announcement, Corporation will hold further consultations with the individual packers and reconsider the data above referred to on or before the 
[ordinal number of day]day of [name of month], the Corporation will make a second announcement of price or prices that Corporation believes to be a reasonable price, which price or prices may be the same as or different from those previously announced. Such price or prices set forth in the second announcement will be the reasonable price, if such price or prices are accepted within [number of days]days after the second announcement by the requisite packers.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 20. ARBITRATION TO ESTABLISH PRICE
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If the requisite packers do not signify their acceptance of the price or prices announced by Corporation under Sections 18 and 19, those sections will be null and void and of no further effect. The price to be paid under this contract will then be determi
ned by three arbitrators. The decision of the majority of the arbitrators will be binding on the parties to this contract and will be final and conclusive as to a reasonable price for the then-current crop year.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> The arbitrators will be selected in the following manner: [specification of selection method].
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Within [number of days]days following the appointment of the arbitrators, the arbitrators will meet to conduct a hearing to determine what a reasonable price will be for the current crop year. Within [number of days]days of the close of such hearing, the arbitrators will report their decision, which, when signed by a majority of them, will be final and not subject to review.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 21. DAMAGES FOR FAILURE TO RECEIVE FRUIT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If Packer, for any reason other than a price dispute, fails, neglects, or refuses, without just legal cause, to receive prior to the [ordinal number of day]day of [name of month]of any crop season covered by this agreement any fruit sold under this contract and that Packer is obligated by this agreement to receive, Packer will pay all reasonable damages caused by such failure unless the receiving date is extended by mutual agree
ment of grower-members, Packer, and Corporation.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 22. PAYMENT FOR FRUIT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Unless otherwise agreed upon by grower and Packer, payments to grower-members of Corporation who deliver fruit under this agreement will be made by Packer within [number of days]days after full delivery and establishment of price and on demand for payment by grower-members.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> The division of payments for fruit will be as follows: [percentage of payments due to grower-member]&percnt;%of the payments due on delivered fruit shall be paid directly from Packer to grower-members, and [percentage of payments due to corporation]&percnt;%of the payments due on delivered fruit and the entire service charge, as referred to in Section 25 of this contract, shall be paid to Corporation in accordance with the terms of that section.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If Packer, for any reason, fails to pay for the fruit or any other charges that Packer is obligated by this agreement to pay, either to grower&ndash;-members directly or to Corporation, on the date or dates agreed upon, interest at [percentage rate of monthly interest]&percnt;%per month or any part of the month on the unpaid balance will commence to run immediately on such default.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 23. DEFAULT BY PACKER
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If Packer shall default or fail in the performance of any of its obligations under this contract, Corporation may stop any further deliveries to Packer and may deliver the balance of fruit elsewhere. This right may be exercised at any time although Corpor
ation has permitted deliveries to Packer to continue after such default or failure. Continuance of delivery after Packer's default or failure in the performance of any of its obligations shall not be construed as a waiver of Corporation's right to stop de
liveries. Such delivery of fruit elsewhere shall not be a waiver or release of any liability of Packer for default or failure in performance. Packer may be held liable to Corporation or its grower-members for damages suffered as a result of such default.

--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 24. DEFAULT BY CORPORATION
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If Corporation shall default or fail in the performance of any of its obligations under this contract, Packer may stop any further acceptance of fruit under the contract. This right may be exercised at any time although Packer has accepted delivery from C
orporation members after such default or failure in the performance of any of its obligations under this contract. Continuance of delivery after Corporation's default or failure will not be construed as a waiver of Packer's right to stop receiving. Termin
ation of receiving shall not be a waiver or release of any liability of Corporation for default or failure in performance. Corporation may also be held liable to Packer for damages suffered as a result of the default.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 25. SERVICE CHARGE
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> Packer recognizes that the organization and continued existence of Corporation relieves Packer of the trouble, labor, and uncertainty of soliciting and obtaining separate contracts with individual growers for the purchase and sale of fruit. In considerati
on thereof, Packer shall pay to Corporation, over and above the market price designated in this agreement, a service charge of $[dollar amount of service charge]per ton for all fruit delivered to Packer under this contract and for all fruit delivered by ag
ency growers who are members of Corporation. The service charge shall not be construed to be a part of the purchase price under this agreement.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 26. SALE TO OTHER PACKER
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If, during the terms of this agreement, Corporation sells to any Packer fruit of its grower-members at a price less than the price specified in Sections 16 through 21, Corporation will pay to Packer, on all fruit purchased under this contract, the differe
nce between the price established in this agreement and the lowest price at which Corporation shall make sales to other packers.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 27. DISAGREEMENT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> In case any disagreement arises between the parties to this contract, either as to procedures under or interpretations of disagreement, there shall be an arbitration in the manner and under the conditions provided in Section 20.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 28. PURCHASE AT DIFFERENT PRICE
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> If Packer, during or for any season under this contract, has purchased or has agreed to purchase any fruit from a grower-member of Corporation, from anyone other than Corporation, or from anyone other than a member of Corporation at a higher price or pric
es than established in this agreement in accordance with Sections 16 through 21, either upon the basis of grade or without grades, Packer will pay to Corporation for fruit purchased under this contract the highest price that Packer has paid or has agreed 
topay or shall have paid or shall have agreed to pay for fruit so purchased from anyone.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> In computing the higher purchase price so paid or agreed to be paid, there shall be included any bonuses, premiums, hauling or loading allowances, expenses of special services of any character that may be rendered by Packer or at its expense, and any sums
paid or agreed to be paid by Packer for any other designated purpose than payment of purchase price. Nothing contained in this section shall apply to sales of fruit between packers.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="3"</field> 29. SUPREMACY OF LAW
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> This contract will be deemed modified to the extent necessary to comply with state and federal laws and any order, regulation, or license pursuant thereto and marketing agreement or order under the authority of law.

--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|54|32:52"</field> In witness, the parties have executed this agreement at [place of execution]the day and year first above written.

--para--\*<field>

--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"</field> Distributor may select from among the members of corporation those members whose products [he/she]desires to buy under this contract. Subject to the prior consent and approval of the board of directors of corporation, the selected members may then deliver such products directly to Distributor.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 2. PRICES
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"</field> Distributor shall pay to corporation for all dairy products sold and delivered to [him/her]by or through corporation not less than the minimum class prices set forth in the marketing agreement and order for the [name of marketing area]marketing area, State of New York, which [OPTIONAL: agreement was approved by [name of approver] and]became effective [effective date of agreement], and all amendments thereto. A copy of that marketing agreement and order is attached and made a part of this contract. Any new marketing order or amendment to the present order that affects this contract will become effective as to this contract when such new agreement or amendment becomes effective. If the present marketing agreement and order is terminated and not immediately
replaced by a new agreement and order, the price to be paid for dairy products sold and delivered under this contract will be mutually agreed on between the parties to this contract.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 3. INABILITY TO PERFORM
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"</field> In case of any cause beyond the control of either party that shall render it impossible for corporation to deliver or Distributor to handle or dispose of dairy products to be sold or received under this agreement, no liability for nonperformance of this a
greement caused hereby will be incurred during the existence of that cause. In the case of a short supply of the dairy products covered by this agreement, corporation agrees to prorate its production on a percentage of sales basis with every buyer of dair
y products. In the case of its inabilities to supply dairy products from locally purchased sources, corporation will attempt to purchase such products for Distributor's account from outside sources.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 4. ACCOUNTS, RECORDS, AND INSPECTIONS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"</field> Distributor agrees to keep complete and accurate records and accounts of all dairy products received by [him/her]
or at [his/her/its]plant during the term of this agreement, showing the source, quality, quantity, and disposition thereof, with dates, together with accurate summaries thereof, and to render such accounts and records to corporation at the time of or prior to the settlemen
t of accounts between the parties. Corporation will have full opportunity to check the sufficiency and accuracy of such records, accounts, and summaries and shall be permitted to have one or more representatives on the premises of Distributor where such dairy products are received, handled, processed, and prepared for sale and delivery at all times, with authority to take inve
ntories; to examine the salespersons' daily load and return sheets and all other records and memoranda covering road sales; to check samples of cream; and to take samples of milk and cream from any cans or containers on the premises.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 5. BUTTERFAT TESTS
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"</field> The payment for all milk will be based on the average of not less than [number of separate butterfat tests]separate butterfat tests of each producer's delivery during each month, conducted by an independent laboratory acceptable to Distributor and corporation. Corporation and Distributor will each pay one-half of the cost of such tests. Both Distributor and c
orporation agree to accept as final the average of the [number of samples]samples taken by the laboratory as a basis of settlement. Corporation may check weights and butterfat tests at Distributor's plant at all times.
--para--\*<field>fi.lvl="1"</field> 6. ACCOUNTING AND PAYMENT
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"</field> Distributor will render to corporation not later than the [ordinal number of day]day of each month an accounting of all dairy products purchased during the preceding month. Payment for all such dairy products will be made directly to corporation daily on estimates furnished by corporation, subject to adjustment based on complete bill
ing at the end of the month. Any underpayment or overpayment resulting from such daily payments as compared to the total billing for the month will be made good by the party liable therefor immediately on notice of such liability. Final adjustment as a result of ordered adjustment of receipts at sale shall be settled immediately on determination of the ordered adjustment.

Where not settled by the agreement, the price to be paid is a reasona
ble price at the time for delivery if: (a) nothing is said as to price; (b) the price is left to be agreed by the parties and they fail to agree; or (c) the price is to be fixed in terms of some agreed market or other standard as set or recorded by a thir
d person or agency and it is not so set or recorded.

--para--Notes to Form--para-- --para--Tax Notes 
--para--\*<field>
p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|63|32:60"</field> Among the many requirements imposed on cooperatives is that of giving notification regarding distributions to the patrons. \*<field>st.ref.id="I05PANJ"</field> 26 U.S.C.A. &s;\'a71388(a)(2). The usual manner of handling this is to incorporate a provision into the bylaws similar to the above and then giving patrons a copy of the bylaw along with the letter of notification described. This must be done before a contract is entered into because
, under the Code, the obligation to pay patronage dividends must have existed before the organization received the amount so paid, meaning before the transaction is entered into with the patron.
--para--\*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|63|32:60"</field> The need for the bylaw to which reference is made in this provision arises with respect to qualified written notices of allocation. See \*<field>x.ref.id="I05MHIN"</field> &s;\'a732:6.

<field>form.du="0"</field> \*<field>form.fid="Ia3a03260181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3"</field> \*<field>p.ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|67|32:62"</field> Corporation may exercise all packing, marketing, grading, and inspection or other powers and rights granted in this agreement to it and perform all obligations herein assumed by it, through [name of central sales agency]as a central sales agency. Producer acknowledges that corporation has or will become a member of such central sales agency and has or will contract with the central sales agency to deliver all of the products handled by it to the central sales agency for
packing and marketing. Producer agrees that corporation may contract with the central sales agency for these purposes and may agree to pool the products delivered under this agreement with products of a similar grade and quality delivered by similar corp
orations under marketing agreements substantially similar to this; the proceeds of this agreement will be divided ratably according to deliveries from such corporations and will be distributed to the grower members as above provided.
